Kind           : XC_EXCHANGE_CORRELATION
Description 1  : CAM version of LDA0
Family         : XC_FAMILY_LDA
   func_id: 178                 
References     :       kind: XC_EXCHANGE_CORRELATION  
                    comment: CAM version of LDA0
                 
                 This is a range-separated functional, based on the error function kernel.
                 
                 Functional has a range-separation constant  0.333,
                 and 25.0% short-range and 50.0% long-range exact exchange,
                 
                 Reference(s):
                   *) M. A. Mosquera, C. H. Borca, M. A. Ratner, and G. C. Schatz, J. Phys. Chem. A 120, 1605 (2016)
                      doi: 10.1021/acs.jpca.5b10864
                 
                 Compilation has support for:
                   *) energy
                   *) first derivative
                   *) second derivative
                 
                 Default thresholds:
                 density: 1.000000e-15
                    zeta: 2.220446e-16
                 
                 Functional has no external parameters.
                 
                 To use the functional, the calling program must add in the following terms:
                   *) Short-range (erf) exact exchange, weight = -0.250 omega = 0.333
                   *) Hartree-Fock exchange, weight =  0.500
Dimensionality : 3
Quantities     : 
Other flags    : XC_FLAGS_I_HAVE_ALL
min dens       : 1e-15
min grad       : 0
min tau        : NULL
min zeta       : NULL
init           : NULL
